  - Security hardened. Browse output now has trust boundary markers so agents   
  can distinguish page content from tool output. CDP binds to localhost only.

       2 + * Escape HTML special characters to prevent XSS when                 
         +inserting                                                             
       3 + * user-controlled or API-provided strings into innerHTML.

       5 +export function escapeHtml(str: string): string {                     
       6 +  return str                                                          
       7 +    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')                                           
       8 +    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')                                            
       9 +    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')                                            
      10 +    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')                                          
      11 +    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');                                          
      12 +}

      40 +    /// Close the database connection. Safe to call when no           
         +queries are in flight.                                                
      41 +    /// After closing, the connection is invalid until                
         +reopen() is called.                                                   
      42 +    pub fn close_connection(&self) {                                  
      43 +        // Drop the inner Connection by replacing with a new          
         +invalid one                                                           
      44 +        // This releases the file lock and closes the handle          
      45 +        drop(self.conn.lock().unwrap());                              
      46 +    }                                                                 
      47 +                                                                      
      48 +    /// Reopen the connection to the current db_path. Must be         
         +called after close_connection()                                       
      49 +    /// and after the database file has been replaced (e.g.,          
         +after a restore).                                                     
      50 +    pub fn reopen_connection(&self) -> Result<()> {                   
      51 +        let mut conn_guard = self.conn.lock().unwrap();               
      52 +        // Release the old connection first                           
      53 +        *conn_guard = Connection::open(&self.db_path)                 
      54 +            .context(format!("Failed to reopen database at            
         +{:?}", self.db_path))?;                                               
      55 +        conn_guard.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON", [])            
      56 +            .context("Failed to enable foreign keys on                
         +reopen")?;                                                            
      57 +        Ok(())                                                        
      58 +    }                                                                 
      59  }                                                                     
      60

     # FSRS v0.2.0 ‚ÄĒ Spaced Repetition Algorithm Upgrade

     ## Overview

     Replace the current simplified SM-2 implementation with FSRS (Free
     Spaced Repetition Scheduler) to reduce review count while maintaining
     equivalent retention.

     **Current SM-2 implementation:**
     - Stage-based intervals: 10min ‚Üí 1day ‚Üí 3day ‚Üí 7day ‚Üí 14day ‚Üí mastered
     - No ease factor adjustment
     - `correct_streak` increments but doesn't affect scheduling
     ‚Ä¶ +202 lines (ctrl+o to expand)
